The toilet is a domestic smart toilet. The smell in the bathroom is disgusting. There is also dirty dirt on the edge of the basin. The lighting in the room is very dim and looks dirty.
The towels don't look white, they just look low. The water in the shower ranged from light rain to moderate rain, but the moderate rain had not yet arrived.
The pillows are all latex pillows, and the charging plugs are on the bedside table. After all, the hotel is newly opened.
The sofa also looked dark and unclean.
The service at the front desk is a bit plain and unprofessional.
Breakfast was average. No impression, no interest in taking pictures.
The location is pretty good, only a ten-minute walk from Vientiane City.
The weirdest thing is that the gym and swimming pool actually charge a fee. When I went back and looked at the page, there was indeed an introduction, but the fonts were very small. Easy to miss. This charge is very undignified. Budget airline feel.
The whole experience of the entire hotel is only four stars, not as good as the four-star Hilton and Courtyard.
There is no need to improve, it cannot be improved. It is recommended to assign it directly to four stars.
